  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_13b8cb4b-9e72-45fb-94d6-faa34dbcb5a4'
      });

  <span id="freeText5388968391601763172" style="display:none">To want what you’re not supposed to have…<br /><br />She is only nineteen.<br /><br />She is his new stepfather’s daughter.<br /><br />She is still naïve and innocent due to spending the last three years taking care of her sick mother.<br /><br />But for twenty-four year old Rush Finlay, she is the only thing that has ever been off limits. His famous father’s guilt money, his mother’s desperation to win his love, and his charm are the three reasons he has never been told no.<br /><br />Blaire Wynn left her small farmhouse in Alabama, after her mother passed away, to move in with her father and his new wife in their sprawling beach house along the Florida gulf coast. She isn’t prepared for the lifestyle change and she knows she’ll never fit into this world. Then there is her sexy stepbrother who her father leaves her with for the summer while he runs off to Paris with his wife. Rush is as spoiled as he is gorgeous. He is also getting under her skin. She knows he is anything but good for her and that he’ll never be faithful to anyone. He is jaded and has secrets Blaire knows she may never uncover but even knowing all of that…<br /><br />Blaire just may have fallen too far.</span>

<a href="/questions/254513-can-anyone-recommend-a-book-or-an-author">Can anyone recommend a book or an author similar to Abbi Glines&#39; style?</a>
</div>

<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_254513'><a id="like_count_community_question_254513" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/254513?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">6 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F16070903-fallen-too-far">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/28057010-avidreader1412"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1484068087i/28057010._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/28057010-avidreader1412">Avidreader1412</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Kirsty Moseley (Nothing left to lose, The boy next door, Always you) / Jennifer L Armentrout (Lux series, Covenant, Wait for you series, Etc.) / Wendy<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Kirsty Moseley (Nothing left to lose, The boy next door, Always you) / Jennifer L Armentrout (Lux series, Covenant, Wait for you series, Etc.) / Wendy Higgins (Sweet Evil) / Penelope Douglas (Fall away series)/ Colleen Hoover (Hopeless, Slammed, Maybe Someday, Ugly Love. <br /><br />These are a few very known authors that are Favorites of mine. They're go to authors. They have their own individual style of writing. If you're talking about drop dead gorgeous guys that are some what of a jerk, but change for her. You want to read an INTENSE love that makes your heart melt. Start with anyone of these authors. I think if you love Abbi you'd love them as well. I do. =D<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<div id="review_553113217" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/553113217" />
    <a title="Ceilidh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3229028-ceilidh"><img alt="Ceilidh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1422140120p2/3229028.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/553113217?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ceilidh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ceilidh" href="/user/show/3229028-ceilidh">Ceilidh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553113217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17066953688021580397">I think I should just give up trying with New Adult literature. So far, the genre has offered none of the maturity or complexities of the liminal period between teen years and full-on adulthood, instead preferring what merely amount to college age erotic romances with a hefty side dish of misogyny. Indeed, the frequency with which sexist portrayals of women and relationships appear throughout works labelled New Adult suggests that the pair go hand in hand. While “Fallen Too Far” didn’t reach the</span>
  <span id="freeText17066953688021580397" style="display:none">I think I should just give up trying with New Adult literature. So far, the genre has offered none of the maturity or complexities of the liminal period between teen years and full-on adulthood, instead preferring what merely amount to college age erotic romances with a hefty side dish of misogyny. Indeed, the frequency with which sexist portrayals of women and relationships appear throughout works labelled New Adult suggests that the pair go hand in hand. While “Fallen Too Far” didn’t reach the despicable lows of “Thoughtless”, it did come pretty close thanks to its incredibly unsettling portrayals of women and relationships.<br /><br />Let’s start with one issue this book presents that I think represents a real disconnect from the contemporary world it claims to depict. Blaire moves from Alabama to Florida to live with her father after the death of her mother, with nothing but $20 in her pocket and a rusty old vehicle. She needs a job to make enough money to get a place for herself. The book is set in 2012 America. We currently live in a world of falling living standards, rising unemployment and a widening gap between the working and middle classes. This applies not only to USA but to most of what is known as the developed world. Blaire is a 19 year old high school dropout with a GED and some brief experience in a couple of after school jobs. Within one day of moving to a completely strange place, she has a well-paying job at a country club, where she is frequently given $50 and $100 tips. She literally walks into this place, says she wants a job and is given one with barely any questions asked. This bugged me for a number of reasons, the main one being that it was insultingly unrealistic. The defenders of New Adult keep talking about how this burgeoning genre has such amazing potential to depict real-life situations that modern young people face every-day, from the personal to the political. Glines took the cheapest route possible with what could have been an interesting twist on the contemporary drama. Unemployment and money troubles are huge issues for my generation, and those stories are dying to be told, so seeing the heroine have it all handed to her so easily (and really? $100 tips?) felt like a real slap in the face. I’ve talked before about how YA and romance tend to fetishise wealth, and “Fallen Too Far” does this to some degree. While it’s made explicit to us that the country club regulars are all lecherous old men or “jealous sluts”, the designated love interest Rush is conveniently very wealthy and will never have to worry about money. <br /><br />Once again, we have another New Adult book where Those Other Women fall into one camp of characterisation – bitches and sluts. If they’re not unreasonably jealous of the beautiful and perfect gun toting virgin Blaire, they’re throwing themselves over Rush or begging for sex constantly. Even side characters, such as country club worker Darla, seem to have nothing but sex on the brain, as she tells Blaire to essentially sex herself up for tips. The virgin/whore complex is rampant throughout. Every single woman in this book who isn’t the heroine is shamed in some manner, be it by the heroine herself or the men around them. It’s the laziest characterisation imaginable and it’s also horrifyingly sexist, particularly when coupled with the male characters of the story, who seem to be nothing but walking erections. Every man in this book except for Blaire’s father leers at her, openly proposition her and make it very clear what they want to do to her. Not only are women seen as objects throughout this novel, every woman aside from Blaire is portrayed as one. <br /><br />Unfortunately, not even the sainted heroine makes it out of this damaging double standard unscathed. Yet again, we have another NA romance where the heroine is simultaneously infantilised and sexualised by the designated love interest. Rush is very controlling (of course), getting angry when Blaire turns down his offer of food (and of course we have another romantic hero who is obsessed with getting the woman to eat, although shudder to think any of these authors would ever portray the heroine as anything other than the stereotypical skinny size), and talking about Blaire as if she’s an object. He’s obsessed with other men touching her or wanting to touch her because apparently they don’t deserve to touch her. The book also includes the delightful line “Your pussy is mine” (to paraphrase it, I didn’t write it down for obvious reasons). The sex scenes are as awful as you imagine them to be, chock full of cringe-worthy dialogue about how hot, tight and deep the sexual experience is. You’re not drilling for oil, Rush, you’re having sex, and being “so in the moment” that you forgot to put a condom on makes you a fuckwit, not a romantic. The “romance” is more lust-based than anything else (of course), with no discernible reason given for why they’re so dramatically in love other than they’re both gorgeous (of course). It seems to come from nowhere in the beginning – Rush goes from being cold and showing absolutely no interest in his step-sister to telling her to stay away to throwing her against a wall in lust to getting angry when others flirt with her at her place of work. It was exhausting, but not as exhausting as the pathetically weak attempts at plotting, characterisation and grammar. <br /><br />I don’t care if your book if self-published. If you let it out into the real world and charge money for it, there is no excuse for sloppy grammar and spelling. There weren’t just one or two slips. There were countless examples of this sloppiness. I don’t know who is editing Glines’s work, if anyone is, but it needs to be sorted out. If you want to call yourself a professional author, you need to act professional.<br />The dialogue is sloppy and predictable, ticking off all the expected boxes of New Adult angst and all-consuming lust (because I refuse to call what these books portray love). The attempts at ambiguity and tension fail miserably because everything is so obvious. There is absolutely no reason for any of the supposed deep dark secrets of Rush and his “bitchy” “spoiled brat” sister Nan to be kept secret. They’re kept secret solely to push forward the bare threads of a plot. The deliberate withholding of information for no reason other than it needs to be withheld for there to be a story is incredibly sloppy writing. When the “cliff-hanger” ending is revealed, we’re left with nothing but a weak excuse for a cash-in sequel. <br /><br />It’s not just that this so-called contemporary romance is unrealistic and chooses the easy way out over tackling the real world issues of our generation. It’s not just that it’s badly written and terribly edited. It’s not just that there are spelling errors and misplaced punctuation and pacing issues. It’s not just that it’s incredibly sexist, romanticised yet another controlling and unhealthy relationship, all the while shaming women in a way that made my skin crawl. It’s not just that the sex scenes were a mixture of laughable dialogue, irresponsibility and sheer boredom. It’s not just all those things. It’s that “Fallen Too Far”, for all its genre in its sexism, laziness, internalised misogyny and sloppiness, is what we’ve now come to expect from New Adult literature. It exemplifies exactly why this genre has failed to meet its most basic potential. All these books, from “Fallen Too Far” to “Beautiful Disaster” to “Thoughtless”, make me feel a little bit dirty. There is something seriously wrong with normalising stuff like this as romantic and sexy. “Fallen Too Far” was detestable. <br /><br />Avoid. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17066953688021580397" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_429092404" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429092404" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429092404?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429092404" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer535619097021837356"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393516i/757627._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> <b> “Blaire, I’m not a romantic guy. I don’t kiss and cuddle. It’s all about the sex for me. You deserve someone who kisses and cuddles. Not me. I just fuck, baby.“ </b></i> <br/><br/><b> Aaaaaaaahhh amazing book but holy cliffhanger!<br/>I need book #2!<br/>Right. Freaking. N O W !<br/>But O.M.G. I loved it! </b><br/><br/>This was my first Abbi Glines book. Ever. How I’ve managed to read this long and NOT read one of her book is a still a complete mystery too me. Her books feel almost like some sort of rite of passage as a reader. Everyone is al</span>
  <span id="freeText535619097021837356" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393516i/757627._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <b> “Blaire, I’m not a romantic guy. I don’t kiss and cuddle. It’s all about the sex for me. You deserve someone who kisses and cuddles. Not me. I just fuck, baby.“ </b></i> <br><br><b> Aaaaaaaahhh amazing book but holy cliffhanger!<br>I need book #2!<br>Right. Freaking. N O W !<br>But O.M.G. I loved it! </b><br><br>This was my first Abbi Glines book. Ever. How I’ve managed to read this long and NOT read one of her book is a still a complete mystery too me. Her books feel almost like some sort of rite of passage as a reader. Everyone is always talking about them and now I know why!! <br><br>I absolutely loved it, cliffhanger and all! A deliciously angsty bad-boy-meets-innocent-girl forbidden romance.<br><br>It was one of those books that I pretty much inhaled in one sitting and made me get all growly whenever someone tried to interrupt me.<br><br>Half a page in and I was grinning from ear to ear and yup, everything I’ve heard about Abbi Glines’ writing is true. Its addictive and catchy making the pages just fly right by. Its funny at times but will also pull the rug out from under you in a heart beat with its twist. And its got this really easy-to-read and yet delightfully angsty feel to it!<br><br>After Blaire’s twin sister was killed in a car crash her father left their home, not even returning when Blaire’s mother died of cancer. Now, with no money, no home and no where else to turn, Blaire is sent to live with him and his new wife. But when she shows up he's run off to Paris and instead is her new step-brother….. Rush Finlay.<br><br>Rush was just absolutely delicious. With silver eyes, tattoos and a tongue piercing, he pretty much just oozed sex appeal. Add that to his cocky yet charming, hot/cold, mysterious, man-whoring bad-boy attitude, and how protective he got of Blaire the more he fell for her and you’ve really got quite the recipe for yum. I just love that kind of character. Makes my heart flutter every time.<br><br><i> <b> “You don’t want to know me. You may think you do but you dont. I promise.” </b></i> <br><br>But holy introduction! Literally, the first few times we see him, he’s having sex. Each time with a different girl!! He goes through girls like water, but yet he won’t touch Blaire. He wants her with every fiber of his being but doesn’t feel worthy of her. And he’s holding a big secret that could tear them apart if Blaire finds out.<br><br><i> “I can’t touch you. I want to so damn bad it hurts like a motherfucker but I can’t. I won’t mess you up.” </i><br><br>The whole set up just gave the book that wonderful angsty feeling that makes you desperate for answers. Are they? Will they? Wont they? AND WHAT WAS THE BIG SECRET??? ohhhhhhhh I just needed to know!!<br><br>Blaire was such a likeable heroine. No matter what life threw at her, she was the type of girl who would find the silver lining and work through it. I loved her can-do attitude to everything. On one hand, she was this sweet yet naive, oh-so innocent country girl and on the other she was this tough-as-nails chick who’d really been put through the ringer by life but didn’t let it get her down. Oh, and she actually pulled a gun on someone. Twice!! Yeah, pretty hard not to like her <br><br>I loved watching them fall for each other. It wasn’t smooth – no insta-love here. But the more time they spent around each other, the harder it was to deny the pull they both felt. And when they finally gave in, oooooh I felt it! I loved it! I loved them together. And holyyyy can Ms. Glines ever write a kiss! Yeah… I’m totally addicted!<br><br><i> <b> “Don’t go getting shy on me now. ‘Cause baby, before the night is over you will be naked in my bed.” </b></i> <br><br>I enjoyed this book right from the start – it probably was sitting at a very happy 4 star rating but somewhere around 70% suddenly my heart was just POUNDING and I couldn’t flip the pages fast enough. Definitely a 5 star feeling if you know what I mean!<br><br>I mean… OHHH MYYY GODDD!!!!!<br><br>The bedroom!!<br><br>The party! Gah! and she wasn’t… but he was… and then… just.. ohhh the angst!<br><br>And then the snail tray thing and his reaction!<br><br>Ooooo then the <i> “test me” </i> thing… *SHIVERS*<br><br>Then <i> “Mine. This is mine.” </i><br><br>The big reveal!! Gah! My heart just broke!!!!<br><br>And then the CLIFFHANGER!!!! I kept flipping the last page over and over again as if somehow it would magically make more words appear!<br><br>I NEED THE NEXT BOOK! Now now NOWWWWWW! But ooohhh I loved this one! I really did! So much!!<br><br><i> <b> “His eyes never left mine. I held his gaze. I could see the storm in his eyes. I knew he was confused. I could even see the fear. Then there was the love. I saw it. The fierceness in his eyes. I believed it. I could see it clearly. But it was too late now. The love wasn’t enough. Everyone always said that love was enough. It wasn’t. Not when your soul was shattered.” </b></i> <br><br>I really think fans of "Beautiful Disaster" will love this book.<br><br>Abbi Glines, once my heart recovers, you have yourself a new fan!<br><br>Now I know a lot of you want to know about the cliffhanger. Yes, I’ll be honest, its brutal. (No, it has nothing to do with cheating.) But I’ll live. Ok, I may be biting my nails until the sequel “Never Too Far” come out on March 12th, but I’m really happy I read this book. It was a quick read and definitely became a fav. I can’t wait to read the rest of Blair and Rush’s story!<br><br>4.5 – 5 stars!!<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393516i/757628._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="535619097021837356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_429079365" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429079365" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429079365?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429079365" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9887391617606952010">*<b>4 Stars</b>*<br/><br/><i>Fallen Too Far</i> was an <b>addictive</b> read! The story picked up momentum immediately and never once faltered in its intensity.  Abbi has done an amazing job in taking a commonly used, but highly sought after plot—<i>sexy bad-boy meets innocent virgin good-girl</i>—and transforming it into something unique and genuine. <br/><br/>After having lost everything important to her, Blaire reluctantly heads to her estranged father's house in search of shelter while she gets her life back on track.  What she encounters</span>
  <span id="freeText9887391617606952010" style="display:none">*<b>4 Stars</b>*<br><br><i>Fallen Too Far</i> was an <b>addictive</b> read! The story picked up momentum immediately and never once faltered in its intensity.  Abbi has done an amazing job in taking a commonly used, but highly sought after plot—<i>sexy bad-boy meets innocent virgin good-girl</i>—and transforming it into something unique and genuine. <br><br>After having lost everything important to her, Blaire reluctantly heads to her estranged father's house in search of shelter while she gets her life back on track.  What she encounters there instead is a sexy, arrogant step-brother and a  buried secret that will rock the foundation of her very world, once revealed. <br><br>Blaire and Rush have a smoldering connection that becomes evident instantly. Once again, this author proves that she can create and sustain sexual tension like no other—and the steam factor is off-the-damn-charts incredible! With many romance novels, I find that the numerous love scenes tend to become over-played and monotonous—doing nothing to enhance the actual story. The opposite is true for this author; her scenes are fun and fresh, wonderfully descriptive and uncontrollably toe curling! <br><br>The plot twist was an interesting and surprising addition. I always love when a story can throw a curve ball that I didn't see coming and I appreciated how this bend in the plot was tackled; believable and not over-the-top. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Everyone always said that love was enough. It wasn't. Not when your soul was shattered.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>A lot of readers are worried about this story's cliffhanger and I can only speak for myself when I say that it's an understandable one and doable, for the most part. That said, I'm very happy that wait for book two will soon be over! Very sweet and sexy read!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Extremely steamy!<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Initial tension, sexy bickering, passionate connection.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Brooding, arrogant alpha. Sweet but strong heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Quick paced, addictive story with a twist. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Engaging and fun. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> Moderate but doable. <br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Follow up, continuing books in series. <br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

</i> ~Blaire<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/f70193c1-1cc5-4887-8965-85601efa25ea_zps7ee6e160.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393561i/757736.jpg" alt=" photo f70193c1-1cc5-4887-8965-85601efa25ea_zps7ee6e160.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Blaire has experienced lost on every level and with her mothers recent death she finds herself in need of her fathers help. The one person she has come to not be able to rely on in her life. Her dad walked out on her and her mother years ago. But you know the old adage <i>desperate times call for desperate measures.</i> And right now Blaire is desperate. <br><br>After her mothers death she had to sale everything of value including her grandmothers home in which she lived in Alabama. <br><br>Her father has since remarried and moved to Florida. Once Blaire arrives at his new home she is surprised by what she finds; and by who she finds. Rush. Blaire had no clue that she had a stepbrother. She also had no clue that her dad was living it up in a swanky beach house with his new wife and stepson. But that's not the kicker... The kicker that leaves her even more bewildered is when she finds out that her dad is out of the country with his wife. When he knew damn well she was on her way to see him.<br><br><br>Rush is not at all very welcoming to Blaire. He puts her in a room under the stairs that is used by the maid. He makes her feel as if she is of no importance and that he must deal with her until he hears from her dad. But Blaire has her own plan. Get a job then get the hell out of the beach house as soon as humanly possible.<br><br><br>Rush is a playboy. The son of a rock star and he lives out his role to the fullest. Though Rush may play cool he is not however as immune to the sweet and innocent Blaire as he led her believe. In fact she get's completely under his skin.<br><br><i>
  <b>“You aren’t what I expected. I wish you were. It’d be so much easier,”</b>
</i> ~Rush<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/c390b9a4-9f7a-4a6d-8f1f-e07460ff8aa1_zpsbc8c121f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393561i/757737.jpg" alt=" photo c390b9a4-9f7a-4a6d-8f1f-e07460ff8aa1_zpsbc8c121f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"The innocence in your eyes screams at me. I want to peel every inch of your clothing off and bury myself inside you but I can’t."</b>
</i> ~Rush<br><br>And although her tries to fight it..he can't.<br><br><i>
  <b>“I don’t want you under those damn stairs. I hate it. But I can’t move you up here. I’ll never be able to stay away from you. I need you safely tucked away,”</b>
</i> ~Rush<br><br><br>And as much as Blaire tries to fight her attraction to Rush she finds it damn near impossible to not want him. In. Every. Way.<br><br><i>
  <b>'I needed to find someone else to focus on. Someone that wasn’t Rush. Someone that was available. It was the only way I was going to keep from falling too far.'</b>
</i> ~Inner monologue of Blaire<br><br>Rush holds back and Blaire starts to get the feeling that he has secrets. Soon Lines are crossed as they give in to temptation.<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/tumblr_mherchuG0L1r9jtuao1_500_zps6c2d7e28.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393561ra/757738.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mherchuG0L1r9jtuao1_500_zps6c2d7e28.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/44842e22-f0f4-4b21-a93d-c7b98b0df99d_zpsdba0b27b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393561i/757739.jpg" alt=" photo 44842e22-f0f4-4b21-a93d-c7b98b0df99d_zpsdba0b27b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"I don’t know what this is that is going on between us but from the moment I laid eyes on you I knew you were going to change my world. I was terrified. The more I watched you the more you drew me in. I couldn’t get close enough.”</i>
</b> ~Rush<br><br>When the truth finally surfaces from the secrets Rush has kept....<br><b> ALL HELL BREAKS LOOSE.</b><br><br><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>This book left me emotionally spent. I loved Blaire she was so sweet and kickass at the same time. She was beautiful inside and out and I think that is one of the reasons why Rush could not help but fall in love with her.<br><u>The writing</u> was good. The story had a great build to the final scene. The pacing was natural and the romance was<i> SO TASTY</i>. The story also had great secondary characters. I found Woods, Grant and Bethy very entertaining.<br><br>Dear Readers <br>I gave this book 4 stars because it held my attention, gave me lot's of angst, a sexy romance, great secondary characters and a finale that will leave you <b>STUNNED</b>. If you enjoy mature YA and/or NA then this book is for you so<b> READ IT</b>!<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Lovable and Sexy<br>Writing Style- Good with nice pacing and witty phrases <br>Plot/Storyline- It will pull you in and not let go til the last page<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I loved it!!! Read it!!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3008936905435827362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Miss H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h"><img alt="Miss H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475977422p2/15490946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478444635?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss H" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h">Miss H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=smutty-reads">smutty-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=douch-canoe-hero">douch-canoe-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=please-fire-your-editor">please-fire-your-editor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=alpha-fail">alpha-fail</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=absolute-frustration">absolute-frustration</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=insufferable-mc">insufferable-mc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478444635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8606824713523249902">2.5 stars. I didn't love it, but I certainly didn't hate it, either.<br/><br/>One of my main gripes about this book was the horribly bad editing. It was distracting and took away from the story. And the writing style certainly didn’t help. It was a little pedestrian, if I’m being honest. There were missing commas, run-ons, and sentences that read awkwardly enough to give me pause. <br/><br/>Don’t even get me started on the difference between action tags and dialogue tags, and how to properly punctuate them. You can</span>
  <span id="freeText8606824713523249902" style="display:none">2.5 stars. I didn't love it, but I certainly didn't hate it, either.<br><br>One of my main gripes about this book was the horribly bad editing. It was distracting and took away from the story. And the writing style certainly didn’t help. It was a little pedestrian, if I’m being honest. There were missing commas, run-ons, and sentences that read awkwardly enough to give me pause. <br><br>Don’t even get me started on the difference between action tags and dialogue tags, and how to properly punctuate them. You can’t speak an action. A period is needed as a separator between the action and the dialogue, not a comma.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470502743ra/19936044.gif" width="400" height="217" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Moving on.<br><br>I felt like there was far too much telling and not enough showing. Show me, don’t tell me, as the saying goes. I could’ve done without all the internal musings, especially when Blaire would just repeat something in her mind that had already been said aloud by someone else, as if further explanation was needed. That kind of redundancy is exasperating. It’s like, yeah, I’m not stupid. I got it the first time, thanks.<br><br><u>Rush:</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397645ra/767476.gif" width="400" height="172" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396818ra/765240.gif" width="400" height="213" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400990ra/777593.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, I can’t with him. He was an asshole, a liar, and a manwhore, none of which helped to endear him to me. I just didn’t see the appeal. He went out of his way to make sure that Blaire understood that she was unwanted, that he was merely tolerating her presence. He made false assumptions about her and used those same assumptions to excuse away his atrocious behavior. He had no business pursuing anything with Blaire, not with all the secrets he was keeping. And as much as he claimed to want to stay away from her, he didn’t try very hard.<br><br><u>Blaire:</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397296ra/766448.gif" width="400" height="216" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For a smart girl, she sure was dumb. In the beginning, I thought she was strong, independent, and kind of feisty, but all of that changed rather quickly. She became too much of a martyr. She had no backbone and was a doormat for most of the book, although she redeemed herself somewhat at the end. I just didn’t understand her attraction to Rush, and her constant fawning over his good looks was an irritant I could’ve done without. I mean, this man-child publicly kicked her out of his house on the first night she met him, but all she could focus on was how beautiful he was.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470503065ra/19936067.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470503065ra/19936068.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Blaire fell too hard, too fast. Their love was rushed, for lack of a better word, and felt superficial to me. It didn't make sense.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8606824713523249902" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4528297501382181589"><br/><b>
  <i>She is a beautiful damsel in distress....<br/><br/>But is he her knight in shining armour ??</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>He might be,he might not.</b><br/><br/><i>It does not matter because she is falling for his charms, falling for his caring side.Falling for the rush only he can give her.She is falling for this intriguing and very bad boy.</i><br/><br/><b>And she might just have......<br/><br/>.....FALLEN TOO FAR!!</b><br/><br/>--------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/>Now,first of all,allow me to vent my anger and frustration.....<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Nan</u>
</b>--<br/><br/>Can't you get rid of all the ve</span>
  <span id="freeText4528297501382181589" style="display:none"><br /><b>
  <i>She is a beautiful damsel in distress....<br /><br />But is he her knight in shining armour ??</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>He might be,he might not.</b><br /><br /><i>It does not matter because she is falling for his charms, falling for his caring side.Falling for the rush only he can give her.She is falling for this intriguing and very bad boy.</i><br /><br /><b>And she might just have......<br /><br />.....FALLEN TOO FAR!!</b><br /><br />--------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Now,first of all,allow me to vent my anger and frustration.....<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Nan</u>
</b>--<br /><br />Can't you get rid of all the venom and see that she is innocent?<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Abe</u>
</b>--<br /><br />I hate you.You are a pathetic excuse for a lover,husband and father.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Rush</u>
</b>--<br /><br />You idiot!!!Why the hell didn't you tell her all that sooner? Damn...don't worry,I still love you.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Blaire</u>
</b>--<br /><br />Damn girl,don't do this!!!<br /><br /><br />**sigh** I'm done.Sorry,I usually rant in the end,but by now nearly everyone has already read this book.So I figured it won't hurt.<br /><br />------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />I liked this one.And now I know why everyone raves about this.This is good.<br /><br />I like that Blair is strong,independent and does not whine.Though she is a bit naive too.I can say that I admire her loyalty.But I hope she will listen to others once she calms down.<br /><br />Now Rush,I am a sucker for guys like this.I mean who isn't.<br /><br /><b>Hot,bad boys with an even badder attitude!!</b><br /><br />So,<b>Rush Crush Club</b><br /><br /><br />The story was fast paced and easy to read.Though I would have appreciated a little more insight on the characters and a greater bonding with them.<br /><br />---------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>The Story--</i>
</b><br /><br />Blaire is nineteen.She had devoted her life to taking care of her sick mother.Her father had left them years ago.So after her mother passes away,she is left with nothing.With no money or family,she calls her father and asks for a place to stay till she can get a job.<br /><br />She arrives at <b>Rosemary Beach,Florida</b>.And instead of her father,meets with......<b>her stepbrother,Rush.</b><br /><br /><br />And then Readers....<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Eyes meet, oh my, sparks fly, heat level booms.....</b>
</i><br /><br />As I said it's good,very good.<br /><br />------------------------------------------------<br /><br />And yes,I have to say that I'm lucky.....<br /><br />Never Too Far is out!!<br /><br /><b>So I'm going to rush to get Rush....</b><br /><br /><br />That's all for now,Readers.<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_430750712" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/430750712?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny Levine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny Levine" href="/user/show/12673270-jenny-levine">Jenny Levine</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12673270-jenny-levine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer430750712" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer676483458775672806">First of all, let me just get this out of my system.<br/><br/><b> FUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUU!!!<br/>WHAT IN THE WORLD?!!! </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/413023.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, now that I've let it all out, off to my review...<br/><br/><b> Fallen Too Far... </b> <i> Hmmm... </i> The book is as beautiful as it's cover. The story is about <b> Blaire </b> who after the demise of her mother, seeked help from the person who hasn't been there for her her whole life, her father. When she came to the address he sent, guess what? Her father's not there! The one who welcomed her (or not?) is <b> Rush Finla</b></span>
  <span id="freeText676483458775672806" style="display:none">First of all, let me just get this out of my system.<br><br><b> FUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUU!!!<br>WHAT IN THE WORLD?!!! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/413023.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, now that I've let it all out, off to my review...<br><br><b> Fallen Too Far... </b> <i> Hmmm... </i> The book is as beautiful as it's cover. The story is about <b> Blaire </b> who after the demise of her mother, seeked help from the person who hasn't been there for her her whole life, her father. When she came to the address he sent, guess what? Her father's not there! The one who welcomed her (or not?) is <b> Rush Finlay </b>, her father's stepson and the owner of the house. But living with him isn't going to be easy. And thus, their story begin...<br><br>Reading this has been an emotional one. I've fallen too far and too deep...in love with this book. I admit at the first chapter, I was like <i> Team Grant!!! </i> Haha! He was the one who first met Blaire and I really thought there's gonna be a love triangle. He was just so sweet, the complete opposite of Rush. I don't like Rush at first but when the story progressed, he turned out to be a great person. He's a rockstar's son, he's sexy and possessive/protective of Blaire so what's not to love, right? Of course, there's a villain in the story who goes by the name of <b> Nan </b> who is such a BITCH, I just wanna slap her and her posse for giving Blaire such a hard time <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ She has her reasons though, which will be revealed at the last chapter of the book, and that's when I understood her  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Sometimes, it's Blaire I wanna put some sense into. On the first scene of the book when he pulled out her gun and pointed it at Grant, I was like <i> HELLS YEAH! A badass heroine! </i> But, reading the next chapters, I realized, she isn't that tough. I know she's been through a lot, but I just want to see her fighting back or make a snarky comebacks/comments or just be a bitch and not allow anyone to just kick her ass like that. Oh well, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she did stood up for herself though at nearly the end part of the book  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Okay, moving on... I love how the story went on, at first, Rush ignoring his feelings for Blaire, but when he couldn't take it anymore, WOW!!! These two are a perfect pair! I love their moments together (and love scenes), which really showed Rush's sweet side. <b> MAJOR SWOON FEST!!! </b><br><br><i> “You naked in my bed is even more unbelievably beautiful than I thought it would be… and trust me I’ve thought about it. A lot.”<br><br>“I thought you weren’t a cuddler, Rush,” I said as he ran his nose along my neck and inhaled loudly.<br>“I wasn’t. Only with you Blaire. You’re my exception,” he whispered then tucked my head under his chin and pulled the covers up over us.<br><br>“Talk. We are going to talk first. I want to see you smile and laugh. I want to know what your favorite show was when you were a kid and who made you cry at school and what boy band you hung posters of on your wall. Then I want you naked in my bed again.” </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393783ra/758231.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And when everything is going out so well for the couple...<b> BOOM! </b> The inevitable happened! Secrets and LIES have been revealed, and it was one helluva drama-filled scene. So emotional. I'm just like:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393783ra/758232.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mean, NOOOOO! I know it was bound to happen, but not like that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393783ra/758233.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It took me a long time to write this review because I still can't get over the last chapter of the book. It was just so intense and tear-jerking. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <i> “Talk. Hurry. I want you gone,” I told him.<br>Rush flinched from my words. I would not allow myself to feel for him. I couldn’t.<br>“I love you.”<br>No. He was not saying that. I shook my head. No. I was not hearing this. He did not love me. He couldn’t. Love didn’t lie. </i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393783ra/758234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> WARNING: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There is no HEA in this book. Not yet anyway  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><blockquote> <b> <i> “He wasn’t what sent me running. He was what made me want to stay.” </i><br><br>Their story isn’t over… </b> </blockquote><br>This is the type of book you'll hate to love. You hate that it ended that way...but you still love it anyways. ;)<br><br><b> 4.5 STARS! </b><br><br>Now, off to find a <i> standalone </i> book with an HEA to read.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_477042211" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/477042211" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/477042211?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=freaking-cliffhanger">freaking-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer477042211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3160636944499566629"><br/><b>4.5 ENTERTAINING BUT HIGHLY EMOTIONAL STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>Fallen Too Far</b> was my very first book by Abbi Glines and I already know it won't be my last...<br/><br/><b>Blaire --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400786i/777140.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Rush --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400786i/777141._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i><u>She's</u> a young, unexperienced girl who's been hurt more than once by the people she loved.<br/><br/><u>He's</u> a typical bad boy...tattooed, pierced and a different girl every night.<br/><br/><u>They</u> are each others stepbrother and stepsister and therefore a recipe for disaster... (or not).</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>When I first started reading <i>Fallen Too Far</i> I expected it to be an easy, fun stor</span>
  <span id="freeText3160636944499566629" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 ENTERTAINING BUT HIGHLY EMOTIONAL STARS.</b><br><br><b>Fallen Too Far</b> was my very first book by Abbi Glines and I already know it won't be my last...<br><br><b>Blaire --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400786i/777140.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Rush --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400786i/777141._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i><u>She's</u> a young, unexperienced girl who's been hurt more than once by the people she loved.<br><br><u>He's</u> a typical bad boy...tattooed, pierced and a different girl every night.<br><br><u>They</u> are each others stepbrother and stepsister and therefore a recipe for disaster... (or not).</i>
</b><br><br><br>When I first started reading <i>Fallen Too Far</i> I expected it to be an easy, fun story without too much drama and at first, it was just that. But then there was suddenly a highly emotional turn of events that managed to keep me hooked until the very last page. Needless to say, I was unable to put it down and ended up finishing the book in one sitting...<br><br><b>Fallen Too Far</b> is the story of the nineteen year old girl named <b>Blaire Wynn</b>. For the past three years of her life she's been taking care of her sick mother without the help of anyone but herself. Her father left their family after Blaire's twin sister died in a car accident and he hasn't returned ever since. Now that her mother passed away and Blaire has no money left because of all the medical bills, she has no one to turn but her father... <br><br>He allows her to stay at his house in Florida but when Blaire arrives there, her father has run off to Paris with his new wife. Instead, Blaire is faced with her new stepbrother...<b>Rush Finlay</b>. It's immediately obvious that Rush and Blaire are from two completely different worlds; he's spoiled, a little condescending and he's used to always getting what he wants. Now all he wants, is Blaire but he also knows he might not be the right kind of guy for her...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Blaire, I'm not a romantic guy. I don't kiss and cuddle. It's all about the sex for me. You deserve someone who kisses and cuddles. Not me. I just fuck, baby. You aren't meant for someone like me. I've never denied myself something I want. But you're too sweet. This time I have to tell myself no." ~ Rush</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>They try to stay away from each other as much as possible but they both know the attraction between them isn't easy to resist. And as much as Rush tries to play it cool, Blaire slowly but surely manages to get under his skin.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The problem was that you fascinated me. I'll admit I was immediately drawn to you because you're gorgeous. It was breathtaking. Then...then I got to know you, I was hypnotized by your laugh. It was the most amazing sound I'd ever heard. You were so honest and determined. You didn't whine or complain. You took what life handed to you and worked with it. I wasn't used to that. Every time I watched you, every time I was near you I fell a little more." ~ Rush</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400786i/777142.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a while they do fall for each other. Hard. But just when things seems to be going in the right direction...<b>Holy revelations!</b> Secrets and lies are revealed that might shatter their entire lives apart...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"His eyes never left mine. I held his gaze. I could even see the fear. Then there was the love. I saw it. The fierceness in his eyes. I believed it. I could see it clearly. But it was too late now. The love wasn't enough. Everyone always said that love was enough. It wasn't. Not when your soul was shattered." ~ Blaire</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400786i/777143.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>It was fun reading how the tough guy Rush started falling more and more for the sweet and innocent Blaire. At first, I honestly didn't like his character all that much. He was just a typical bad boy who thought he was better than Blaire just because he had more money. But after a while we got to see a whole other side of him and I started to like him more and more (plus the guy was HOT, no getting around that fact...). Blaire, on the other hand, I loved her from the start. At times she was insecure and a little naïve, other times she has no problem with going to a honky-tonk or with pulling a gun on someone. Overall, they were both very refreshing and interesting characters that made reading the story even better.<br><br>As for the ending of the story, I have to warn you, it's kind of dramatic and it will leave you desperate to find out what happens next. After the book endedI just felt like <i>"This is it?? Really...this is how it's going to end??"...</i><br><b>First there was disbelief -</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400786ra/777144.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><b>Then there was despair -</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/448759.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><b>And after that there was nothing...</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400786ra/777145.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>Although I have to admit, it was also a good thing the story ended that way, because now I'm even more anxious to read the next part of this very entertaining series.<br><br>I can't wait to find out how the story of Rush and Blaire continues...because we already know their story isn't over yet.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[For now, they haven't gotten their HEA yet, but hopefully they will in the next part of the series! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He wasn't what sent me running. He was what made me want to stay."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And I already know that for the next few days/hours, I'll be anxiously awaiting <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17029526.Never_Too_Far__Too_Far___2_" title="Never Too Far (Too Far, #2) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Never Too Far</a>...<br><br>P.S.: Future readers won't have to worry about the cliffhanger anymore because the second book will be released very soon! (26 February 2013)<br><br><br>****<br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3160636944499566629" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489511911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1674524197383967553">This is me officially giving up on Abbi Glines' books<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/throw%20book%20gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402633ra/782727.gif' alt='Rigoletto Throwing a Book Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Did you read that GR community? <br/><br/>I. GIVE. UP.<br/><br/>I just cannot seem to find what's so amazeballs about her books when all I find in them is just beautiful. RICH. people.<br/><br/>The main character, Blaire, was just <i>so</i> stupid I can't even decribe it. And Rush, the male lead, was <i>so</i> full of shit. I wanted to kick his ass during the <i>entire</i> book<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/pissed%20gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402633ra/782728.gif' alt='pissed gif Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>My God, I hated this book. I did. And <i>nothing</i> will change my mind.<br/><br/>This is just one big hot mess. Starting with</span>
  <span id="freeText1674524197383967553" style="display:none">This is me officially giving up on Abbi Glines' books<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/throw%20book%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402633ra/782727.gif" alt="Rigoletto Throwing a Book Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Did you read that GR community? <br><br>I. GIVE. UP.<br><br>I just cannot seem to find what's so amazeballs about her books when all I find in them is just beautiful. RICH. people.<br><br>The main character, Blaire, was just <i>so</i> stupid I can't even decribe it. And Rush, the male lead, was <i>so</i> full of shit. I wanted to kick his ass during the <i>entire</i> book<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/pissed%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402633ra/782728.gif" alt="pissed gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My God, I hated this book. I did. And <i>nothing</i> will change my mind.<br><br>This is just one big hot mess. Starting with Rush's mood swings that had me all mad and confused and followed by Blaire's stupidity of falling for a guy who has sex with a different girl every night. But that's the normal part of the story.<br><br>Blaire <i>SAW</i> Rush have sex with another gir. Like, <i>STARED</i> . That's normal, right?<br><br>No?<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/creepy%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380377862ra/733233.gif" alt="it's creepy Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the ending was a big, fat WTF.<br><br>I don't really want to say too much because, you know, spoilers and all that. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1674524197383967553" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer12886532394880516997"><b>4 Secrets, Lies & Rush Finlay Stars<br/><br/><i>“Talk. We are going to talk first. I want to see you smile and laugh. I want to know what your favorite show was when you were a kid and who made you cry at school and what boy band you hung posters of on your wall. Then I want you naked in my bed again.”</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778582._SX540_.png' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What happens when your world crumbles around you? A car accident took away her twin sister.</span>
  <span id="freeText12886532394880516997" style="display:none"><b>4 Secrets, Lies &amp; Rush Finlay Stars<br><br><i>“Talk. We are going to talk first. I want to see you smile and laugh. I want to know what your favorite show was when you were a kid and who made you cry at school and what boy band you hung posters of on your wall. Then I want you naked in my bed again.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778582._SX540_.png" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What happens when your world crumbles around you? When you are all alone in the world, hopeless and despaired?<br><br><b>Blaire Wynn</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778583.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The nineteen year old girl has lost everything. A car accident took away her twin sister. She lost her mother to cancer, after sacrificing her future taking care of her. And now she has to turn to her deadbeat, coward father to find a place a stay, a new start in her life.<br><br>But life deals her another unexpected hand. Instead of her father she finds his stepson. <br><br><b>Rush Finlay</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396441i/764180._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="620" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>“He’s the only child of the famous drummer for Slacker Demon, Dean Finlay. His parents never married. His mother, Georgianna, was a groupie back in the day."</i>
</b><br><br>Rush is tormented of his own demons. A bad boy, womanizer, cynical bastard that tries to hide a heart full of hurt and vulnerability. Mysterious, perfect, wounded and confusing man. <br><br>He wants her but he is afraid that he will taint her, ruin her and that she will find out the secrets they are harbouring and they will destroy the fragile balance she managed to maintain.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I can’t touch you. I want to so damn bad it hurts like a motherfucker but I can’t. I won’t mess you up. You’re… you’re perfect and untouched. And in the end you would never forgive me.”</i>
</b><br><br>They can't deny the sizzling chemistry and the strong bond that forms between them. A love stronger than both of them but will it be stronger than the lies and deceit?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688400.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy freaking Hell... A beautiful emotional story that destroyed me and broke my heart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778584._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WHAT IN THE NAME OF GOD HAPPENED???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370947ra/723939.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nan, I hate you! I completely loathe you. I have an aversion to uppity bitches, but you made me allergic to them...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401265ra/778585.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then the ending kinda destroyed me...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/529352.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/475491.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I admire every single one of you that survived this cliffhanger!!! Already started the next...<br><br><b>
  <i>“Whatever we had is over. It died the minute I walked downstairs and realized the world I’d always known was a lie.” <br><br>"The love wasn’t enough."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778586.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>My initial reaction to the cliffhanger, that proved life-saving...<br><br>December 2013</i><br><br>I was warned about this book:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778587.gif" width="220" height="214" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Never Too Far (Fallen Too Far #2)<br><br>Expected publication: March 12th 2013 <br><br><b>So.... to save my sanity, I'll read them together after March 13th 2013!!!!!!!</b><br><br><i>REVISED at 04/13/13 to post full review.</i><br><br><b>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429018025" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429018025?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=author-abbi-glines">author-abbi-glines</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429018025" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer430749134822345334"><b>Abbi Glines does IT again!! <br/><br/>I love this story and the possibilities for future books are endless!!!</b><br/><br/>My Cast Photos <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393505i/757610._SX540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393505i/757611._SX540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>After burying her mother, Blaire packs her old truck and heads for some much needed help from her estranged father. She hasn’t been in contact with him since he walked out on her and her mother and remarried. She has no idea that he is living high on the hog with a new family. <br/><br/>Blaire’s father didn’t even have the decency to be there to greet her when she arrived. He is away with hi</span>
  <span id="freeText430749134822345334" style="display:none"><b>Abbi Glines does IT again!! <br><br>I love this story and the possibilities for future books are endless!!!</b><br><br>My Cast Photos <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393505i/757610._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393505i/757611._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>After burying her mother, Blaire packs her old truck and heads for some much needed help from her estranged father. She hasn’t been in contact with him since he walked out on her and her mother and remarried. She has no idea that he is living high on the hog with a new family. <br><br>Blaire’s father didn’t even have the decency to be there to greet her when she arrived. He is away with his wife on vacation. Yep a real winner! She is coldly greeted by her stepbrother Rush and is offered to sleep in a closet under the stairs in this mansion of a home. Rush also gives her two weeks to stay. Yep can you feel the warmth --- but there is chemistry and it’s strong.<br><br>Rush Finlay is gorgeous playboy who is very deep and tortured. He is very sexual and is drawn to Blaire. FYI- he has piercings and tattoos. Too bad he is keeping a secret. <br> <br><b>
  <i>"Blaire, I'm not a romantic guy. I don't kiss and cuddle. You deserve someone who kisses and cuddles. Not me. I just fuck, baby. You aren't meant for someone like me."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”I push people away Blaire. It’s a protective mechanism for me. But I don’t want to push you away.”</i>
</b><br><br>Blaire is a strong, beautiful girl both inside and out. She is a hard worker who never ever pities herself and you just have to respect her for that alone! She finds her strength in the love that her mother gave it keeps her secure, like a foundation. <br><br>Poor Blaire is treated a bit like Cinderella living under the stairs of the mansion and working for the elite at the country club. The chemistry is bubbling between Rush and Blaire. Rush soon finds that he can no longer resist her. Even though, Rush’s sister Nanette is an evil biotch towards Blaire, the couple’s attraction to each other turns into so much more.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I had fallen too far. I was in love with Rush Finlay.”</i>
</b><br><br>Then there’s Woods, I REALLY like him as well! He is Blaire’s boss at the Country Club. I’m looking forward to reading more about him as well as Bethy a friend Blaire made at work. <br><br>But back to this secret... it seems that EVERYONE knows but Blaire. Even her boss seems to know something WTF right? This secret is looming for most of the book and once you find out what it is things deteriorate between Blaire and all who resides in Rosemary, Florida.<br><br><b>
  <i>I didn’t have a past. I didn’t have a foundation.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Everyone always said that love was enough. It wasn’t. Not when your soul was shattered.”</i>
</b><br><br>Where will Never Too Far take us?<br><br>Here’s some of my wishes and ideas: <br><br>Woods comes to Alabama because he didn’t get to say goodbye. He talks Blaire into returning to Florida and explains that she has made a lot of friends and is missed terribly by everyone including him. <br><br>Woods offers her her job back at the club so she can have her own place, possibly with Bethy? <br><br>I would love for Grant to get more of a storyline.<br><br>I have a feeling that this is only the beginning and we are in for another great series by the talented Abbi Glines!</span>
  <a data-text-id="430749134822345334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer17896456585208638432">Abbi has done it to me again!!! I LOVED THIS STORY!!!! Such great characters that pull you in and make you root for them or hate them with such passion. March can not come fast enough!!!<br/><br/>My Rush:<br/><a href='http://s1300.beta.photobucket.com/user/Becca_Manuel/media/65299_3361019203937_1208560392_n_zpsea3f3c65.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396441i/764180._SY540_.jpg' alt='Rush - Fallen Too Far' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

<div id="review_429869141" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429869141" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429869141?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
