        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429869141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6626124062927756236">Wait, another book with an "innocent" girl and a guy who's played everyone? Isn't this like every other Glines book (at least the 6 or so others I've read)? I get formulas, but there comes a point where you have to write a DIFFERENT character type in order to prove that you are more than a one-trick pony. How about flipping this for once and giving us the experienced girl with the inexperienced guy?<br/><br/>Sigh. I was going to read this because I do like the sexual tension that Glines creates, but now I</span>
  <span id="freeText6626124062927756236" style="display:none">Wait, another book with an "innocent" girl and a guy who's played everyone? Isn't this like every other Glines book (at least the 6 or so others I've read)? I get formulas, but there comes a point where you have to write a DIFFERENT character type in order to prove that you are more than a one-trick pony. How about flipping this for once and giving us the experienced girl with the inexperienced guy?<br><br>Sigh. I was going to read this because I do like the sexual tension that Glines creates, but now I don't know...<br><br>I even broke out the happy keys for <i>Because of Low</i> because I thought we headed in a positive direction. Do I need to get myself a new key?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393641i/757870.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/179852-katie-babs?shelf=gag-worthy-book">gag-worthy-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer546846551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2510617793945422789">When I finished reading, this is a perfect example of how I felt:<br/><br/><a href='http://www.gifbin.com/984442' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382251ra/739986.gif' alt='funny gifs' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/> For those who loved Fallen too Far (Fallen Too Far #1), it might be best for you to disregard this review because my reaction to this latest by Abbi Glines has me less than happy. Actually more like, WTFOMGBBQ did I read? This book is the perfect example of what is wrong with New Adult and the path it’s taking as a genre or a literary category. I will start by saying that Glines does have an engaging writing style. I can see w</span>
  <span id="freeText2510617793945422789" style="display:none">When I finished reading, this is a perfect example of how I felt:<br><br><a href="http://www.gifbin.com/984442" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382251ra/739986.gif" alt="funny gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> For those who loved Fallen too Far (Fallen Too Far #1), it might be best for you to disregard this review because my reaction to this latest by Abbi Glines has me less than happy. Actually more like, WTFOMGBBQ did I read? This book is the perfect example of what is wrong with New Adult and the path it’s taking as a genre or a literary category. I will start by saying that Glines does have an engaging writing style. I can see why she has a big fan base. The heroine Blaire is wonderfully written and a character you want to root for, but the other characters in this tale are a big, big problem mainly because they're all stereotypes and are written as wretched, horrible people. Ever see the movie, Cruel Intentions and how nasty the majority of those characters are and you don’t feel one ounce of sympathy for any of them? That's what Fallen Too Far is. <br><br>Blaire is all alone in the world. Her mother has died, and because she has no place to go, she’ll live with her father she despises because he turned his back on them and acts as if they never existed. Because Blaire is poor, and yet a hard worker, she is put down and ridiculed by the richy-rich people she must interact with, mainly her father's new stepson, Rush, who is a well known man slut to the max. Rush is a walking STD and makes no qualms about it. When Blaire meets him, he's rude and crude to her. Throughout the story Blare seems him disrespecting women, as in he sleeps with them and throws them out after he gets his jollies off. We see this on the page and it's not assumed or subtly shown. Rush is the type of man who needs a therapist because it's obvious he has such rage against women. <br><br>Here’s a perfect example of what I’m talking about. The morning after Blaire's arrival, she meets one of the many girls Rush sleeps with:<br><br>“There you are. I missed you in bed this morning.” A soft female coo came from behind me. Curiosity got the better of me and I turned around. A girl in nothing but her bra and panties was snuggling up to Rush’s side and running a long pink fingernail down his chest. I couldn’t blame her for wanting to touch that. I was pretty tempted myself.<br><br>“It’s time for you to go,” he replied taking her hand off his chest and stepping away from her. I watched as pointed in the direction of the front door.<br><br>“What?” she replied. The confused expression on her face said she hadn’t been expecting this.<br><br>“You got what you came here for, babe. You wanted me between your legs. You go it. Now I’m done.”<br><br>The cold hard flatness in his voice startled me. Was he serious?<br><br>“You’re kidding me!” the girl snapped and stomped her foot.<br><br>Rush shook his head and took another drink from his cup.<br><br>“You are not going to do this to me. Last night was amazing. You know it.” He girl reached out for his arm and he quickly moved it out of the way.<br><br>“I warned you last night when you came to me begging and taking off your clothes that all it would ever be was one night of sex. Nothing more.”<br><br><br>Keep in mind that Rush is going to end up being Blaire’s love interest, the same man who has sex with girls and one night stands without a care.This is the man Blaire will fall in love with and choose as her soul mate. You'd think Blaire would stay far away from him, and make friends with the nice guys she works with and have a romance with one of them. Nope. Blaire is attracted to Rush regardless of his psychotic and bullying ways that are really more what a villain entails. But no matter because Blaire sleeps with Rush in very descriptive and erotic type love scenes that are very angry for both parties involved. The purpose is for them to find physical release with no emotional attachment. The sex between them is full of rage and greed, and shows how really pathetic these two are when all is said and done.<br><br>At one point Rush tries to rape Blaire (this is subjective on my part, so I welcome the discussion from other readers who agree or disagree), or I guess some readers would say he pulled a forced seduction on Blaire because even though she’s angry with him, and at first refuses him, her body responds to him and she finds her climax and then wants more. This scene reminds me of the almost rape scene (in a truck also) that begins Tammara Webber's Easy. Funny how Buck, who tries to rape Jacqueline, the heroine of that story, is the nasty villain, but when Rush does the same to Blaire, he's the hero, the love interest and one the reader is supposed to sympathize with and wants Blaire to have her HEA with. That scene was vile and disgusting. Again I ask, what was the point? To show how destructive and hot Rush's and Blaire's lust is for one another and think it’s amazing? To try and compare them to Heathcliff and Cathy’s sick and destructive love in Emily Bronte’s Wuthering Heights? I refuse to say love when it comes to Rush and Blaire because these two can't love one another. They're both disturbed and extremely unhealthy for one another. Rush chips away at Blaire’s soul until there is nothing sweet and genuine left. The Blaire at the end of this tale is a shell of her former self because Rush has sucked the life out of her via explosive orgasms, including the lies she unravels from her father and the ones Rush tells her.<br><br>Glines at no times gives us an adequate example why Blaire would fall for Rush and why the reader should expect these two to be together and be fine with it. I lost respect for Blaire the moment she decides to give into her attraction for Rush "just because". She's lonely and since he's amazing in bed, she'll use him exactly like he uses others.<br><br>Gone Too Far is the complete opposite of what a romance should be. I would stay far away from reading this one. If this is what the future of New Adult is or romance for readers jumping from Young Adult into adult romance, then I'm very saddened. I felt the need to shower after I finished reading this book and wanted to read a book where the heroine and heroine respect one another and share their love in healthy and uplifting ways.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2510617793945422789" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_467258761" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467258761" />
    <a title="Autumn Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review"><img alt="Autumn Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399327915p2/6908049.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/467258761?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autumn Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autumn Review" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review">Autumn Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=beta">beta</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467258761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8586377411020881169">This is one of the hardest reviews I've ever had to write. Why, you ask? Well, I can tell you it might possibly be my favorite Abbi Glines book written, but I don't want to say much and ruin the story for you all. So, I'll give you a few highlights and strongly encourage you to get it. <br/><br/>This book is Blaire's story. I loved this chick the minute she pulled out her gun. Literally. She's strong, smart, independent and loving. But, unfortunately for Blaire, she's had to suffer through some pretty hor</span>
  <span id="freeText8586377411020881169" style="display:none">This is one of the hardest reviews I've ever had to write. Why, you ask? Well, I can tell you it might possibly be my favorite Abbi Glines book written, but I don't want to say much and ruin the story for you all. So, I'll give you a few highlights and strongly encourage you to get it. <br /><br />This book is Blaire's story. I loved this chick the minute she pulled out her gun. Literally. She's strong, smart, independent and loving. But, unfortunately for Blaire, she's had to suffer through some pretty horrific losses in a relatively short time frame. She's looking for support from her father until she can make some money and go out on her own. However, he's not there for her yet again. My heart hurt for her and I really hated her dad for not being there for her. Once you learn more about her story, you will love her even more. You connect with her. You want to be her friend. You want to hug her. When she meets Rush, her life tilts once again. <br /><br />I love all the girls in Abbi Glines' books, but I usually fall for the boys immediately. She knows how to write sexy men. Well, Rush is certainly sexy, but it did take me a while to warm up to him. That said, I trusted that Ms. Glines would win me over....and I was right. It took a while to love Rush, but once I did, it was a big fall. Rush is complex. He's a rock star's son, so he's seen things and done things in his life that are well...pretty experienced. He's loyal to his family though and is a very passionate guy. <br /><br />The relationship that Rush and Blaire have is a bit complicated. As I said before, Rush is very experienced and Blaire is not. (Not to mention the familial obstacles they face.) She has been in a relationship before, but she's never known a guy like Rush. These two have some serious heat together. Without giving too much away, I'll tell you that there are several extremely hot scenes between these two. If you know me at all, you know that I LOVED that! <br /><br />I have to mention the supporting characters. I often make strong attachments to the supporting characters in Abbi Glines' books. In this book I really fell hard for Grant. He is funny and super sweet. I'm rooting for a book for Grant. Of course every story has it's villain, and in this one it's Nan, Rush's sister. She is just plain nasty, but I do understand why. Not that it made me like her any better though. <br /><br />Here's the thing, I had the privilege of watching this story come to life and it's truly amazing seeing an author create a story. This particular story is a little bit different than some of Glines' other books though. Don't fear...you get your romance, swoony guys, and fantastic supporting characters. But, this story is a bit more raw and gritty. I will say that, as the end of this year wraps up and I think of all of the truly great books that have hit my self this year, Fallen Too Far will be among my favorites of 2012. I can't wait for you all to read it! </span>
  <a data-text-id="8586377411020881169" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479987254" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11898081097693786567">Review posted to: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>5 Sensational Stars<br/>Genre: New Adult Contemporary Romance/ very Mature Young Adult Romance <br/>Heat Barometer: 5 out of 5 flames<br/></b><br/>This is the first book in a new series and it was…Spectacular! Fireworks! Explosions! Abbi Glines writes the steamiest, mature young adult romances that I have read. She is a “drop everything else and move her book to the top of the list” author for me, and I definitely haven’t been disappointed it her latest books. <br/><br/>In <b>Fallen Too Far</b>, t</span>
  <span id="freeText11898081097693786567" style="display:none">Review posted to: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><b>5 Sensational Stars<br />Genre: New Adult Contemporary Romance/ very Mature Young Adult Romance <br />Heat Barometer: 5 out of 5 flames<br /></b><br />This is the first book in a new series and it was…Spectacular! Fireworks! Explosions! Abbi Glines writes the steamiest, mature young adult romances that I have read. She is a “drop everything else and move her book to the top of the list” author for me, and I definitely haven’t been disappointed it her latest books. <br /><br />In <b>Fallen Too Far</b>, the connection and combativeness between the characters was such a turn on. I steamrolled through it at 100 mph, I couldn’t stop, it was that addictive.<br /><br />Rush was <i>designer</i> and Blaire was <i>country</i>. Rush grew up the son of a world famous rock and roll drummer. He was gorgeous and rich with sexy tattoos and piercings on a perfect physique. Blaire was a good girl, she grew up in a normal family setting until her twin sister was killed in a car accident. Her world and family was torn apart and in the end, her normal high school life was a heartbreaking struggle as she took care of her sick mother alone. <br /><br />This book comes out fast with the heartache. I had to swallow my tears many times as Blaire would recount her past tragedies and memories with her mother and her last years of high school. Blaire was a strong and pure heroine. She was a wonderful and caring daughter and she had such pride and innocence that Rush and every male in this book should have been her protector and defender…she deserved it. Rush was the perfect “Jerk” hero, the kind I just love because you know in the end the heroine is going bring out the good in him and it going to be such an adventure until it gets to that point.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>”I don’t kiss and cuddle, I just f*ck baby.”</i>
</b> - and boy did he ever.<br /><br />The chemistry between Blaire and Rush was off the charts and instantaneous. There were a lot of “other women”, jealousy and dirty talking situations that just built the anticipation and sexual tension to a frenzied eruption. What made all this wonderful connection even better was the story. There was lots of mystery and innuendos, twists and turns that I didn’t see coming. The depth and direction led to one heck of a reveal...it could be I was so caught in the sexual fog of Blaire and Rush that I was blindsided.<br /><br />At 93% I kept thinking I hope this isn't a quick ending because the book has been too perfect to just finish it off. Well, heartbreaking cliffhanger is what I got. I found this author just in the last 5 months and 3 of the books I have read from her are solid 5 star reads. I highly recommend her and this series and I CANNOT WAIT UNTIL MARCH 13, 2013 for the sequel.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer431258923" class="readable"

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="erika" class="user" itemprop="url" name="erika" href="/user/show/31424620-erika">erika</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1625976770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1234673758537359645">If you liked this book, good. I'm so happy you liked it. If you decide to read this review, please know that it is not a hate review. This is just my opinion. <br/><br/>I wanted to like this book. I really did. But for me personally, Fallen Too Far is the embodiment of everything wrong with a lot of books in the New Adult genre<br/><br/>The main character, Blair Wynn was infuriating for me. I couldn't stand her. She was just so stupid<br/>And then we have Rush Finlay, who was just as horrible. He was the tortured soul t</span>
  <span id="freeText1234673758537359645" style="display:none">If you liked this book, good. I'm so happy you liked it. If you decide to read this review, please know that it is not a hate review. This is just my opinion. <br /><br />I wanted to like this book. I really did. But for me personally, Fallen Too Far is the embodiment of everything wrong with a lot of books in the New Adult genre<br /><br />The main character, Blair Wynn was infuriating for me. I couldn't stand her. She was just so stupid<br />And then we have Rush Finlay, who was just as horrible. He was the tortured soul type (don't get me wrong here, I have a huge soft spot for these types) but he wasn't the good kind. He was the kind who shoved it in your face as an excuse<br /><br />I feel like I've read this same plot a million times. Girl meets asshole, said asshole doesn't want her around because secretly he's instantly in love with her and he knows this will be a problem, so he is just a dick to her when it suits him but when he wants her, the girl just does what he wants because she is so completely in love with him. Throw in a few jealous girls and a bad home life for both people and you have this book.<br />I'm so over reading this same plot line over and over again and there weren't even any characters that made this book redeemable for me<br /><br />With that being said, if your a fan of this type of book, than this one is for you </span>
  <a data-text-id="1234673758537359645" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_468425820" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468425820" />
    <a title="Bayli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6979410-bayli"><img alt="Bayli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498671323p2/6979410.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468425820?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bayli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bayli" href="/user/show/6979410-bayli">Bayli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=2012">2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6979410-bayli?shelf=romance-new-adult">romance-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468425820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14762530411360343824"><b>The first half of the book I would give around 3.5 but the second half around 4.5- So, I'm going to settle at <i>4 Stars</i></b><br/><br/>Meet Blaire and Rush:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399499i/773178.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Get it giiiirrrrl</i><br/><br/>The first half of the book was just kind of strange to me...<br/>So this new girl, Blair, shows up at her dads house. A father she hasnt seen in about 5 years. Her mother has died of cancer, she has no money after paying for the medical bills, all she has is her truck and $20 in her pocket... So her father says he can stay with him and his NEW wife</span>
  <span id="freeText14762530411360343824" style="display:none"><b>The first half of the book I would give around 3.5 but the second half around 4.5- So, I'm going to settle at <i>4 Stars</i></b><br><br>Meet Blaire and Rush:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399499i/773178.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Get it giiiirrrrl</i><br><br>The first half of the book was just kind of strange to me...<br>So this new girl, Blair, shows up at her dads house. A father she hasnt seen in about 5 years. Her mother has died of cancer, she has no money after paying for the medical bills, all she has is her truck and $20 in her pocket... So her father says he can stay with him and his NEW wife and step kids until she can make enough money to move out. <br><br>Well that's all well and good. Except, he's not even there when she knows up. He's on vacation with his new wife? After his first wife had just died and his daughter needed him? What a piece of shit. <br><br>Anyway. <br>SO here comes Blaire. Country girl, Blaire. She parks in fron of this house with her ancient truck and meets Grant. Now, i really liked Grant- he was sweet and funny- but really she pulled a gun on him? I mean sure that kind of made me laugh and it diesnt really bother me that she did that- mean it made her seem like a badass! However, the gun doesnt really fit with the rest of her personality. <br><br>I think Blair was supposed to be this hardcore country girl that doesnt take shit from anyone- but all I read through out this entire book was her just taking it and doing nothing about it. THAT DROVE ME NUTS. I mean this is the same girl that was trigger happy at the beginning of the book correct?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399499ra/773179.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I dont know, i just think this girl would have had a mouth on her. Would have gone off on these bitches at these parties, etc. But instead she gets all upset and runs away into her hidey hole... Strange, right?<br><br>But what really drives me crazy about Blaire... I mean really just wants me to bang her head against a wall- She knows absolutely nothing about sexuality. I get it- she's a sweet, innocent- virgin. Awesome. Kudos. I'm happy for you... But, come on- a 19 (almost 20) year old woman would know more about her body and about sex that Blaire did. Yes, even though her mom was sick and she had "no time for sex" she still would have known more than she did in this book..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399499ra/773180.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, that's me- whacking Blaire upside the head.<br><br>So that made me feel like she really shouldnt be having sex if she knew <i>that little</i> about her own body and what sex really was. <br><br>I guess i just thought she was a little <b>too</b> innocent. <br><br>Rush annoyed me at the beginning too. Mostly because Blaire and him had barely even spoken- yet they were just so incredibly attracted to one another? There was just this magical pull? I guess I just wish there would have been more conversation between the two of them in the first half of the book...<br><br><b>OKay, I promise I am done bitching- The second half of this book was really good!</b><br><br>The second half gets more interesting. <br>Rush starts to make it a point to keep his eye on Blaire at all times. He becomes really protective of her- and well- I find that extremely hot. <br><br>Blaire starts to be willing to give into her desires to Rush. Even though in the back of her mind- she knows it will never actually work out. She just wants to be with him any way.<br><br>After the honkey tonk.... <br>At this point I'm really loving Rush. He has gone from annoying boy that thinks hes gods gift to the world- to hot boy that cant get enough of the one girl he shouldnt have... I mean that is sexy, right?<br><br>Right.<br><br>Of course- things keep getting in there way. <br><br>Nan, Rush's sister- is a bitch. <br><br>There's a huge secret that I won't give away in this review but it's <b>huge</b>. It envolves Nan. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/502923.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So the entire Nan thing keep getting in the way of Blaire and Rush- until one night they finally seal the mother freakin deal... And it's all hot. <br><br>Rush is so into Blaire at this point- it's ridiculous (in a good way ;)) Dude is totally falling for her. <br><br>Shit goes down......<br>Blaire finds out about the secret.....<br>And the world as she and Rush has known it- has come to a close.......<br>She runs away from it all, from all of them, including Rush, and runs back to her hometown........<br><br><br>Where we are left with a very very painful cliffhanger :( damnit. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14762530411360343824" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_503853627" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503853627" />
    <a title="Marina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13500406-marina"><img alt="Marina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361224250p2/13500406.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503853627?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marina" href="/user/show/13500406-marina">Marina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=delicious-bad-boys">delicious-bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=in-one-word-good">in-one-word-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503853627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1379890165142523442"><b>WHAT IN THE NAME OF ALL CLIFFHANGERS??</b><br/><br/><br/><i>The moment when you realize the book has ended but the story hasn't:</i><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371412ra/724464.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/494522.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/>Ok, I am slightly calmer now. But I really have to say something or I'm probably going to explode.<br/><br/><b>YO PEOPLE.</b> Whether you are fictional or not, <b>STICK BY YOUR CHILDREN'S SIDE.</b> You might be screwed up beyond repair, you might regret your decisions. <b>I DON'T CARE. STICK BY YOUR FAMILY OR GET THE HELL OFF THE FACE OF THE EARTH.</b><br/><br/>Choosing the benefit of one child over the other? And f</span>
  <span id="freeText1379890165142523442" style="display:none"><b>WHAT IN THE NAME OF ALL CLIFFHANGERS??</b><br><br><br><i>The moment when you realize the book has ended but the story hasn't:</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371412ra/724464.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/494522.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><br>Ok, I am slightly calmer now. But I really have to say something or I'm probably going to explode.<br><br><b>YO PEOPLE.</b> Whether you are fictional or not, <b>STICK BY YOUR CHILDREN'S SIDE.</b> You might be screwed up beyond repair, you might regret your decisions. <b>I DON'T CARE. STICK BY YOUR FAMILY OR GET THE HELL OFF THE FACE OF THE EARTH.</b><br><br>Choosing the benefit of one child over the other? And for what? To ease your guilt? To shy away from the responsibility of taking care of a family shattered by pain? <b>WHAT IS WRONG WITH YOU?</b><br><br><b>Blaire.</b> My beautiful girl. An amazing character. A strength and loyalty so fierce that made my chest burst with pride. The love for her mother is so admirable that by the end I was cheering up for her to get the hell out of that family.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“My mother and my sister’s graves are home. I want to be near them. I’ve stood here and listened<br>to y’all tell me my mother was someone who I know she wasn’t. She would have never done what you’re<br>accusing her of. Stay here with your family, Abe. I’m sure they will love you as much as your last one did.<br>Try not to kill any of them,” I spat.<br><br>*****<br><br>I tucked my gun back under the seat and backed out of the driveway. I didn’t look to see if they were all huddled around poor Nannette. I didn’t care. Maybe she’d think twice before she fucked with someone else’s momma. Because, by God, she better never talk bad about mine again.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>And Rush.</b> Dude. I know you dont't exist but you REALLY need to read some more novels. You are a book boyfriend and let's just face it:<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404775i/787975.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_488328006" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/488328006" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/488328006?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488328006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2449850466318990616">I just love when the bad boy 'playa' falls and especially when he doesn't realize he is falling! The sweet part about this story is that you have Blaire who has gone through some horrible things in the past five years: her twin sister dies, her father left and then she alone takes care of her mother who dies of cancer...she can definitely take care of herself! But she wants someone to want to be with her...to share her life and be there for her. Then you have Mr. Bad Boy, son of a rock god, pier</span>
  <span id="freeText2449850466318990616" style="display:none">I just love when the bad boy 'playa' falls and especially when he doesn't realize he is falling! The sweet part about this story is that you have Blaire who has gone through some horrible things in the past five years: her twin sister dies, her father left and then she alone takes care of her mother who dies of cancer...she can definitely take care of herself! But she wants someone to want to be with her...to share her life and be there for her. Then you have Mr. Bad Boy, son of a rock god, pierced, tattooed, money bags and a sex machine who is totally taken by surprise by Blaire. He fights it and fights it hard but when he finally accepts it, he just can't get enough!<br /><br />I was pleasantly surprised by this book several different time. I didn't expect Blaire to be so mature and capable and I didn't expect her love interest to be Rush. I also didn't expect to like him since he was such a jerk in the beginning. There's also a big secret in the story...it's not too hard to figure out but ultimately becomes Rush's undoing. <br /><br />I thought Blaire was doing really well considering what all she had been through. I about died when she had to sleep in the room under the stairs...it certainly gave off a Cinderella vibe! She really has to deal with the separate social classes...not just where she is staying but at work as well. Luckily, she handles herself (and her gun) quite well. <br /><br />Rush was definitely unexpected considering he was such a jerk at the beginning and was having sex out in the open where Blaire would see him! I love how he reacted to Blaire but I didn't like the secret he was keeping. It was funny to see him trying to fight his feelings and losing! <br /><br />There are some other great characters. I really enjoyed Grant, Rush's step brother and had initially thought he would end up with Blaire. Woods really grew on me and I can't quite help but think something else will go on with him in the future. Nan was a total biotch...I know she was pushed in that direction but it was her choice to continue there. I can't help but feel she's going to get hers. <br /><br />There are some good steamy scenes but not as detailed as some adult books. I think I just happened to like them more because of Rush's reactions and his dirty mouth!! <br /><br />The ending is a bit of a clincher and does leave you hanging. My heart went out to Blaire especially at the cemetery and then OMG at the hotel. I don't know who I felt worse for....her or Rush. Thankfully, the next book, <i>Never Too Far</i>, will be out March 12, 2013. <br /><br />Also don't miss out on an excerpt from Rush's POV:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.abbiglines.com/2012/12/special-excerpt-from-fallen-too-far-retold-in-rushs-pov/">http://www.abbiglines.com/2012/12/spe...</a><br /><br />ETA 12/30: Rush's POV when he first meets Blaire...there are spoilers! <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/abbiglinesauthor/posts/276780092444739">https://www.facebook.com/abbiglinesau...</a><br /><br /><br />Favorite quotes:<br /><br />♥ I was hypnotized by your laugh. It was the most amazing sound I’d ever heard.<br /><br />♥ “His eyes never left mine. I held his gaze. I could see the storm in his eyes. I knew he was confused. I could even see the fear. Then there was the love. I saw it. The fierceness in his eyes. I believed it. I could see it clearly. But it was too late now. The love wasn’t enough. Everyone always said that love was enough. It wasn’t. Not when your soul was shattered.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="2449850466318990616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16680213686815460395">~ SIZZZZZLIN' ~ <br/><br/>Abbi Glines, you are my semi-guilty pleasure of the New Adult genre!! AWESOMELY HOT, bad-boy heroes. Explosive chemistry. Detailed and delicious sex scenes. Just enough angst to keep your emotions involved, but not rip your heart out and stomp on it. Woman, you ROCK!! <br/><br/>Fallen Too Far is hot, sexy fun! The hero and heroine, Rush and Blair, set the pages ON FIRE!! Rush is the only son of a famous rock musician, and Blair is the innocent, big-hearted good girl who has sacrificed a lo</span>
  <span id="freeText16680213686815460395" style="display:none">~ SIZZZZZLIN' ~ <br /><br />Abbi Glines, you are my semi-guilty pleasure of the New Adult genre!! AWESOMELY HOT, bad-boy heroes. Explosive chemistry. Detailed and delicious sex scenes. Just enough angst to keep your emotions involved, but not rip your heart out and stomp on it. Woman, you ROCK!! <br /><br />Fallen Too Far is hot, sexy fun! The hero and heroine, Rush and Blair, set the pages ON FIRE!! Rush is the only son of a famous rock musician, and Blair is the innocent, big-hearted good girl who has sacrificed a lot in her life. Let the defilement begin! Bwahahaha;) The story kept moving, and so did Rush and Blair's combustible chemistry. I do wish we could have gotten inside Rush's head a bit, rather than have this written strictly from Blair's POV. AND, the story does end on a cliffhanger. Nevertheless, Fallen Too Far was a very good time:)<br /><br />Abbi Glines writes *super* sexy and unputdownable New Adult (stress on ADULT) stories, and they are books that I often find myself reading more than once because, well, they're just that fun! If you haven't ever read this author, what in the world are you waiting for?!?! Jump on, and ride the Abbi Glines Train of Sexy Good Times with the rest of us addicts!</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The Romance Book Disciple (Samantha)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="The Romance Book Disciple (Samantha)" href="/user/show/3009708-the-romance-book-disciple-samantha">The Romance Book Disciple (Samantha)</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1605673963" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6548608693996692030">4.5 Stars<br/>Ok, so I totally stayed up all night and read this in one sitting! How is that I have never read this series before? And full disclosure, it was my first Abbi Glines book ever! Crazy right? <br/>So, you have your typical over the top angsty teen stuff. Blaire is seriously beaten down-her sister died, her dad abandoned them, then her mom dies and Blaire is all alone. She turns to the father that left her but that only brings Rush and Nan into her life. Drama, drama, drama! <br/>There is a couple t</span>
  <span id="freeText6548608693996692030" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br />Ok, so I totally stayed up all night and read this in one sitting! How is that I have never read this series before? And full disclosure, it was my first Abbi Glines book ever! Crazy right? <br />So, you have your typical over the top angsty teen stuff. Blaire is seriously beaten down-her sister died, her dad abandoned them, then her mom dies and Blaire is all alone. She turns to the father that left her but that only brings Rush and Nan into her life. Drama, drama, drama! <br />There is a couple times they have sex without a condom so I know that is bothersome for my safety gang sisters. There is no cheating once they get together. <br />Full review will be on <a href="http://www.thebookdisciple.com" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Disciple</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6548608693996692030" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+p1k1DDpS/vbe1u9dZ4FwbyYxp0Bo4fdtRniuydRXvhZ1cI9xpE5JbWto07BkqZc7KjYEkruamnajJXBOOc3gA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aL3dgyvDJFxl7bQNbtf84reuq9bwnh8IUSvfWzhkQULL9Xtq3btWggs7TP7a219/5561WbvT8rw+vqghJ9IoOg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer15664131101990087791">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be Britis</span>
  <span id="freeText15664131101990087791" style="display:none">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be British but alas she was born in Alabama. When asked how many books she has written she has to stop and count on her fingers. When she’s not locked away writing, she is reading, shopping (major shoe and purse addiction), sneaking off to the movies alone, and listening to the drama in her teenagers lives while making mental notes on the good stuff to use later. Don’t judge.<br /><br />You can connect with Abbi online in several different ways. She uses social media to procrastinate.<br /></span>
